async function getBathData(url) {
  const r = await fetch(url);

  const m1 = h.match(/"numberOfFullBathrooms":(\d+)/);
  const m2 = h.match(/"numberOfHalfBathrooms":(\d+)/) || h.match(/"halfBathrooms":(\d+)/);

[58] thinking: **Checking bathroom details**

I'm planning to check links to gather information about the number of full bathrooms. I’ll build a function to fetch each link and parse details like price, full, half, total bathrooms, and the description. It seems like I might need to account for card prices too, possibly parsing from meta tags. I'll start with the first ten links until I have at least three full bathrooms. For the server, I think the rate should be okay, so I'll use fetch.

[59] tool_call: repl("Scanning listings for full bathrooms")
<request>
async function summarizeListing(item, idx) {
  const r = await fetch(item.href);
  const h = await r.text();
  const full = Number(h.match(/"numberOfFullBathrooms":(\d+)/)?.[1] ?? NaN);
  const half = Number((h.match(/"numberOfHalfBathrooms":(\d+)/) || h.match(/"halfBathrooms":(\d+)/))?.[1] ?? NaN);
  const total = Number((h.match(/"totalBathrooms":(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)/) || h.match(/"BathroomsTotal":(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)/))?.[1] ?? NaN);
  const price = h.match(/"price":(\d+)/)?.[1] || h.match(/\$(\d[\d,]*)\s*Price/)?.[1];
  const descMeta = h.match(/<meta name="description" content="([^"]*)"/)?.[1]?.replace(/&amp;/g,'&');
  const title = h.match(/<title>(.*?)<\/title>/)?.[1];
  return {idx:idx+1, text:item.text.replace(/\n+/g,' | '), price, full, half, total, title, descMeta, href:item.href};
}
const summaries1 = [];
for (let i=0; i<Math.min(15, listings1.length); i++) {
  const sum = await summarizeListing(listings1[i], i);
  summaries1.push(sum);
  console.log(JSON.stringify(sum));
  if (sum.full >= 3) break;
}
console.log('DONE');
</request>
